<path>/home/ovidiu/Projects/bob/proj/do_export.py</path>
<content>#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os
import shutil
from pathlib import Path

# Define source and destination
source_dir = Path("/home/ovidiu/Projects/bob/proj")
dest_dir = source_dir / "bob-exports"

# Directories and patterns to exclude
exclude_dirs = {'.venv', '.git', '__pycache__', 'node_modules', '.pytest_cache', '.ruff_cache', 'bob-exports'}
exclude_patterns = {'.pyc', '.DS_Store'}

# Create destination directory
dest_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
print(f"Created directory: {dest_dir}")

# Copy files and directories
for item in source_dir.iterdir():
    if item.name in exclude_dirs:
        continue
    
    dest_item = dest_dir / item.name
    
    if item.is_file():
        if not any(item.name.endswith(pattern) for pattern in exclude_patterns):
            shutil.copy2(item, dest_item)
            print(f"Copied file: {item.name}")
    elif item.is_dir():
        shutil.copytree(item, dest_item, 
                       ignore=shutil.ignore_patterns('__pycache__', '*.pyc', '.DS_Store'),
                       dirs_exist_ok=True)
        print(f"Copied directory: {item.name}")

print(f"\nExport completed successfully to {dest_dir}")
print(f"Total items in bob-exports: {len(list(dest_dir.iterdir()))}")
</content>
</write_to_file>
